+enum CampaignResult {
+    Ok(String),
+    BadRequest,
+    NotFound,
+    Conflict,
+    StorageError,
+}
+
+fn create_campaign(body: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CampaignResult {
+    let campaign = match parse_campaign(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CampaignResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if campaign_exists(storage, &campaign.id) {
+        return CampaignResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO campaigns (id, name, dm) VALUES ({}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&campaign.id),
+        sql_string(&campaign.name),
+        sql_string(&campaign.dm)
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CampaignResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_json(&campaign))
+}
+
+fn add_campaign_character(
+    campaign_id: &str,
+    body: &str,
+    storage: &Storage,
+) -> CampaignResult {
+    if !valid_record_id(campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    if !campaign_exists(storage, campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::NotFound;
+    }
+    let character = match parse_campaign_character(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CampaignResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if campaign_character_exists(storage, &character.id) {
+        return CampaignResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO campaign_characters (id, campaign_id, name, level, class_name) VALUES ({}, {}, {}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&character.id),
+        sql_string(campaign_id),
+        sql_string(&character.name),
+        character.level,
+        sql_string(&character.class_name)
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CampaignResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_character_json(&character))
+}
+
+fn add_campaign_event(campaign_id: &str, body: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CampaignResult {
+    if !valid_record_id(campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    if !campaign_exists(storage, campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::NotFound;
+    }
+    let event = match parse_campaign_event(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CampaignResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if campaign_event_exists(storage, &event.id) {
+        return CampaignResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO campaign_events (id, campaign_id, kind, summary) VALUES ({}, {}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&event.id),
+        sql_string(campaign_id),
+        sql_string(&event.kind),
+        sql_string(&event.summary)
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CampaignResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_event_json(&event))
+}
+
+fn read_campaign_state(campaign_id: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CampaignResult {
+    if !valid_record_id(campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    let campaign = match load_campaign(storage, campaign_id) {
+        Ok(Some(value)) => value,
+        Ok(None) => return CampaignResult::NotFound,
+        Err(_) => return CampaignResult::StorageError,
+    };
+    let characters = match load_campaign_characters(storage, campaign_id) {
+        Ok(value) => value,
+        Err(_) => return CampaignResult::StorageError,
+    };
+    let log_count = match campaign_log_count(storage, campaign_id) {
+        Ok(value) => value,
+        Err(_) => return CampaignResult::StorageError,
+    };
+    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_state_json(&campaign, &characters, log_count))
+}
+
+fn parse_campaign(body: &str) -> Option<Campaign> {
+    let id = json_string_field(body, "id")?;
+    if !valid_record_id(&id) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    Some(Campaign {
+        id,
+        name: non_empty_json_string(body, "name")?,
+        dm: non_empty_json_string(body, "dm")?,
+    })
+}
+
+fn parse_campaign_character(body: &str) -> Option<CampaignCharacter> {
+    let id = json_string_field(body, "id")?;
+    if !valid_record_id(&id) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    let level = json_i64_field(body, "level")?;
+    if !(1..=20).contains(&level) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    Some(CampaignCharacter {
+        id,
+        name: non_empty_json_string(body, "name")?,
+        level,
+        class_name: non_empty_json_string(body, "class")?,
+    })
+}
+
+fn parse_campaign_event(body: &str) -> Option<CampaignEvent> {
+    let id = json_string_field(body, "id")?;
+    if !valid_record_id(&id) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    Some(CampaignEvent {
+        id,
+        kind: non_empty_json_string(body, "kind")?,
+        summary: non_empty_json_string(body, "summary")?,
+    })
+}
+
+fn valid_record_id(id: &str) -> bool {
+    !id.is_empty()
+        && id
+            .bytes()
+            .all(|b| b.is_ascii_alphanumeric() || b == b'-' || b == b'_')
+}
+
+fn campaign_exists(storage: &Storage, id: &str) -> bool {
+    query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT id FROM campaigns WHERE id = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(id)
+        ),
+    )
+    .map(|out| !out.trim().is_empty())
+    .unwrap_or(false)
+}
+
+fn campaign_character_exists(storage: &Storage, id: &str) -> bool {
+    query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT id FROM campaign_characters WHERE id = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(id)
+        ),
+    )
+    .map(|out| !out.trim().is_empty())
+    .unwrap_or(false)
+}
+
+fn campaign_event_exists(storage: &Storage, id: &str) -> bool {
+    query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT id FROM campaign_events WHERE id = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(id)
+        ),
+    )
+    .map(|out| !out.trim().is_empty())
+    .unwrap_or(false)
+}
+
+fn load_campaign(storage: &Storage, id: &str) -> Result<Option<Campaign>, String> {
+    let out = query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT id, name, dm FROM campaigns WHERE id = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(id)
+        ),
+    )?;
+    let Some(line) = out.lines().next() else {
+        return Ok(None);
+    };
+    let fields = line.splitn(3, '\t').collect::<Vec<_>>();
+    if fields.len() != 3 {
+        return Err("malformed campaign row".to_string());
+    }
+    Ok(Some(Campaign {
+        id: fields[0].to_string(),
+        name: fields[1].to_string(),
+        dm: fields[2].to_string(),
+    }))
+}
+
+fn load_campaign_characters(
+    storage: &Storage,
+    campaign_id: &str,
+) -> Result<Vec<CampaignCharacter>, String> {
+    let out = query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT id, name, level, class_name FROM campaign_characters WHERE campaign_id = {} ORDER BY rowid;",
+            sql_string(campaign_id)
+        ),
+    )?;
+    let mut characters = Vec::new();
+    for line in out.lines() {
+        let fields = line.splitn(4, '\t').collect::<Vec<_>>();
+        if fields.len() != 4 {
+            return Err("malformed campaign character row".to_string());
+        }
+        characters.push(CampaignCharacter {
+            id: fields[0].to_string(),
+            name: fields[1].to_string(),
+            level: fields[2].parse().map_err(|_| "bad level")?,
+            class_name: fields[3].to_string(),
+        });
+    }
+    Ok(characters)
+}
+
+fn campaign_log_count(storage: &Storage, campaign_id: &str) -> Result<i64, String> {
+    let out = query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM campaign_events WHERE campaign_id = {};",
+            sql_string(campaign_id)
+        ),
+    )?;
+    out.trim().parse().map_err(|_| "bad log count".to_string())
+}
+
+fn campaign_json(campaign: &Campaign) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"id":"{}","name":"{}","dm":"{}"}}"#,
+        json_escape(&campaign.id),
+        json_escape(&campaign.name),
+        json_escape(&campaign.dm)
+    )
+}
+
+fn campaign_character_json(character: &CampaignCharacter) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"id":"{}","name":"{}","level":{},"class":"{}"}}"#,
+        json_escape(&character.id),
+        json_escape(&character.name),
+        character.level,
+        json_escape(&character.class_name)
+    )
+}
+
+fn campaign_event_json(event: &CampaignEvent) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"id":"{}","kind":"{}"}}"#,
+        json_escape(&event.id),
+        json_escape(&event.kind)
+    )
+}
+
+fn campaign_state_json(
+    campaign: &Campaign,
+    characters: &[CampaignCharacter],
+    log_count: i64,
+) -> String {
+    let character_json = characters
+        .iter()
+        .map(campaign_character_json)
+        .collect::<Vec<_>>()
+        .join(",");
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"id":"{}","name":"{}","dm":"{}","characters":[{}],"log_count":{}}}"#,
+        json_escape(&campaign.id),
+        json_escape(&campaign.name),
+        json_escape(&campaign.dm),
+        character_json,
+        log_count
+    )
+}

+enum CampaignResult {
+    Ok(String),
+    BadRequest,
+    NotFound,
+    Conflict,
+    StorageError,
+}
+
+fn create_campaign(body: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CampaignResult {
+    let campaign = match parse_campaign(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CampaignResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if campaign_exists(storage, &campaign.id) {
+        return CampaignResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO campaigns (id, name, dm) VALUES ({}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&campaign.id),
+        sql_string(&campaign.name),
+        sql_string(&campaign.dm)
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CampaignResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_json(&campaign))
+}
+
+fn add_campaign_character(
+    campaign_id: &str,
+    body: &str,
+    storage: &Storage,
+) -> CampaignResult {
+    if !valid_record_id(campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    if !campaign_exists(storage, campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::NotFound;
+    }
+    let character = match parse_campaign_character(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CampaignResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if campaign_character_exists(storage, &character.id) {
+        return CampaignResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO campaign_characters (id, campaign_id, name, level, class_name) VALUES ({}, {}, {}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&character.id),
+        sql_string(campaign_id),
+        sql_string(&character.name),
+        character.level,
+        sql_string(&character.class_name)
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CampaignResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_character_json(&character))
+}
+
+fn add_campaign_event(campaign_id: &str, body: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CampaignResult {
+    if !valid_record_id(campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    if !campaign_exists(storage, campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::NotFound;
+    }
+    let event = match parse_campaign_event(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CampaignResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if campaign_event_exists(storage, &event.id) {
+        return CampaignResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO campaign_events (id, campaign_id, kind, summary) VALUES ({}, {}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&event.id),
+        sql_string(campaign_id),
+        sql_string(&event.kind),
+        sql_string(&event.summary)
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CampaignResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_event_json(&event))
+}
+
+fn read_campaign_state(campaign_id: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CampaignResult {
+    if !valid_record_id(campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    let campaign = match load_campaign(storage, campaign_id) {
+        Ok(Some(value)) => value,
+        Ok(None) => return CampaignResult::NotFound,
+        Err(_) => return CampaignResult::StorageError,
+    };
+    let characters = match load_campaign_characters(storage, campaign_id) {
+        Ok(value) => value,
+        Err(_) => return CampaignResult::StorageError,
+    };
+    let log_count = match campaign_log_count(storage, campaign_id) {
+        Ok(value) => value,
+        Err(_) => return CampaignResult::StorageError,
+    };
+    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_state_json(&campaign, &characters, log_count))
+}
+
+fn parse_campaign(body: &str) -> Option<Campaign> {
+    let id = json_string_field(body, "id")?;
+    if !valid_record_id(&id) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    Some(Campaign {
+        id,
+        name: non_empty_json_string(body, "name")?,
+        dm: non_empty_json_string(body, "dm")?,
+    })
+}
+
+fn parse_campaign_character(body: &str) -> Option<CampaignCharacter> {

+        return None;
+    }

+        id,

     #[test]
+    fn campaign_json_matches_contract() {
+        let campaign =
+            parse_campaign(r#"{"id":"camp-1","name":"Lost Mine","dm":"dm"}"#).unwrap();
+        let character = parse_campaign_character(
+            r#"{"id":"char-1","name":"Nyx","level":3,"class":"rogue"}"#,
+        )
+        .unwrap();
+        let event = parse_campaign_event(
+            r#"{"id":"evt-1","kind":"note","summary":"Nyx scouts the goblin trail."}"#,
+        )
+        .unwrap();
+
+        assert_eq!(
+            campaign_json(&campaign),
+            r#"{"id":"camp-1","name":"Lost Mine","dm":"dm"}"#
+        );
+        assert_eq!(
+            campaign_character_json(&character),
+            r#"{"id":"char-1","name":"Nyx","level":3,"class":"rogue"}"#
+        );
+        assert_eq!(
+            campaign_event_json(&event),
+            r#"{"id":"evt-1","kind":"note"}"#
+        );
+        assert_eq!(
+            campaign_state_json(&campaign, &[character], 1),
+            r#"{"id":"camp-1","name":"Lost Mine","dm":"dm","characters":[{"id":"char-1","name":"Nyx","level":3,"class":"rogue"}],"log_count":1}"#
+        );
+    }

+enum CampaignResult {
+    Ok(String),
+    BadRequest,
+    NotFound,
+    Conflict,
+    StorageError,
+}
+
+fn create_campaign(body: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CampaignResult {
+    let campaign = match parse_campaign(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CampaignResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if campaign_exists(storage, &campaign.id) {
+        return CampaignResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO campaigns (id, name, dm) VALUES ({}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&campaign.id),
+        sql_string(&campaign.name),
+        sql_string(&campaign.dm)
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CampaignResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_json(&campaign))
+}
+
+fn add_campaign_character(
+    campaign_id: &str,
+    body: &str,
+    storage: &Storage,
+) -> CampaignResult {
+    if !valid_record_id(campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    if !campaign_exists(storage, campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::NotFound;
+    }
+    let character = match parse_campaign_character(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CampaignResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if campaign_character_exists(storage, &character.id) {
+        return CampaignResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO campaign_characters (id, campaign_id, name, level, class_name) VALUES ({}, {}, {}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&character.id),
+        sql_string(campaign_id),
+        sql_string(&character.name),
+        character.level,
+        sql_string(&character.class_name)
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CampaignResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_character_json(&character))
+}
+
+fn add_campaign_event(campaign_id: &str, body: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CampaignResult {
+    if !valid_record_id(campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    if !campaign_exists(storage, campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::NotFound;
+    }
+    let event = match parse_campaign_event(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CampaignResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if campaign_event_exists(storage, &event.id) {
+        return CampaignResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO campaign_events (id, campaign_id, kind, summary) VALUES ({}, {}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&event.id),
+        sql_string(campaign_id),
+        sql_string(&event.kind),
+        sql_string(&event.summary)
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CampaignResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_event_json(&event))
+}
+
+fn read_campaign_state(campaign_id: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CampaignResult {
+    if !valid_record_id(campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    let campaign = match load_campaign(storage, campaign_id) {
+        Ok(Some(value)) => value,
+        Ok(None) => return CampaignResult::NotFound,
+        Err(_) => return CampaignResult::StorageError,
+    };
+    let characters = match load_campaign_characters(storage, campaign_id) {
+        Ok(value) => value,
+        Err(_) => return CampaignResult::StorageError,
+    };
+    let log_count = match campaign_log_count(storage, campaign_id) {
+        Ok(value) => value,
+        Err(_) => return CampaignResult::StorageError,
+    };
+    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_state_json(&campaign, &characters, log_count))
+}
+
+fn parse_campaign(body: &str) -> Option<Campaign> {
+    let id = json_string_field(body, "id")?;
+    if !valid_record_id(&id) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    Some(Campaign {
+        id,
+        name: non_empty_json_string(body, "name")?,
+        dm: non_empty_json_string(body, "dm")?,
+    })
+}
+
+fn parse_campaign_character(body: &str) -> Option<CampaignCharacter> {
+    let id = json_string_field(body, "id")?;
+    if !valid_record_id(&id) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    let level = json_i64_field(body, "level")?;
+    if !(1..=20).contains(&level) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    Some(CampaignCharacter {
+        id,
+        name: non_empty_json_string(body, "name")?,
+        level,
+        class_name: non_empty_json_string(body, "class")?,
+    })
+}
+
+fn parse_campaign_event(body: &str) -> Option<CampaignEvent> {
+    let id = json_string_field(body, "id")?;
+    if !valid_record_id(&id) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    Some(CampaignEvent {
+        id,
+        kind: non_empty_json_string(body, "kind")?,
+        summary: non_empty_json_string(body, "summary")?,
+    })
+}
+
+fn valid_record_id(id: &str) -> bool {
+    !id.is_empty()
+        && id
+            .bytes()
+            .all(|b| b.is_ascii_alphanumeric() || b == b'-' || b == b'_')
+}
+
+fn campaign_exists(storage: &Storage, id: &str) -> bool {
+    query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT id FROM campaigns WHERE id = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(id)
+        ),
+    )
+    .map(|out| !out.trim().is_empty())
+    .unwrap_or(false)
+}
+
+fn campaign_character_exists(storage: &Storage, id: &str) -> bool {
+    query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT id FROM campaign_characters WHERE id = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(id)
+        ),
+    )
+    .map(|out| !out.trim().is_empty())
+    .unwrap_or(false)
+}
+
+fn campaign_event_exists(storage: &Storage, id: &str) -> bool {
+    query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT id FROM campaign_events WHERE id = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(id)
+        ),
+    )
+    .map(|out| !out.trim().is_empty())
+    .unwrap_or(false)
+}
+
+fn load_campaign(storage: &Storage, id: &str) -> Result<Option<Campaign>, String> {
+    let out = query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT id, name, dm FROM campaigns WHERE id = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(id)
+        ),
+    )?;
+    let Some(line) = out.lines().next() else {
+        return Ok(None);
+    };
+    let fields = line.splitn(3, '\t').collect::<Vec<_>>();
+    if fields.len() != 3 {
+        return Err("malformed campaign row".to_string());
+    }
+    Ok(Some(Campaign {
+        id: fields[0].to_string(),
+        name: fields[1].to_string(),
+        dm: fields[2].to_string(),
+    }))
+}
+
+fn load_campaign_characters(
+    storage: &Storage,
+    campaign_id: &str,
+) -> Result<Vec<CampaignCharacter>, String> {
+    let out = query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT id, name, level, class_name FROM campaign_characters WHERE campaign_id = {} ORDER BY rowid;",
+            sql_string(campaign_id)
+        ),
+    )?;
+    let mut characters = Vec::new();
+    for line in out.lines() {
+        let fields = line.splitn(4, '\t').collect::<Vec<_>>();
+        if fields.len() != 4 {
+            return Err("malformed campaign character row".to_string());
+        }
+        characters.push(CampaignCharacter {
+            id: fields[0].to_string(),
+            name: fields[1].to_string(),
+            level: fields[2].parse().map_err(|_| "bad level")?,
+            class_name: fields[3].to_string(),
+        });
+    }
+    Ok(characters)
+}
+
+fn campaign_log_count(storage: &Storage, campaign_id: &str) -> Result<i64, String> {
+    let out = query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM campaign_events WHERE campaign_id = {};",
+            sql_string(campaign_id)
+        ),
+    )?;
+    out.trim().parse().map_err(|_| "bad log count".to_string())
+}
+
+fn campaign_json(campaign: &Campaign) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"id":"{}","name":"{}","dm":"{}"}}"#,
+        json_escape(&campaign.id),
+        json_escape(&campaign.name),
+        json_escape(&campaign.dm)
+    )
+}
+
+fn campaign_character_json(character: &CampaignCharacter) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"id":"{}","name":"{}","level":{},"class":"{}"}}"#,
+        json_escape(&character.id),
+        json_escape(&character.name),
+        character.level,
+        json_escape(&character.class_name)
+    )
+}
+
+fn campaign_event_json(event: &CampaignEvent) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"id":"{}","kind":"{}"}}"#,
+        json_escape(&event.id),
+        json_escape(&event.kind)
+    )
+}
+
+fn campaign_state_json(
+    campaign: &Campaign,
+    characters: &[CampaignCharacter],
+    log_count: i64,
+) -> String {
+    let character_json = characters
+        .iter()
+        .map(campaign_character_json)
+        .collect::<Vec<_>>()
+        .join(",");
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"id":"{}","name":"{}","dm":"{}","characters":[{}],"log_count":{}}}"#,
+        json_escape(&campaign.id),
+        json_escape(&campaign.name),
+        json_escape(&campaign.dm),
+        character_json,
+        log_count
+    )
+}
+

     let monster = match parse_monster(body) {
         Some(value) => value,
@@ -1762,6 +2141,37 @@

     #[test]
+    fn campaign_json_matches_contract() {
+        let campaign =
+            parse_campaign(r#"{"id":"camp-1","name":"Lost Mine","dm":"dm"}"#).unwrap();
+        let character = parse_campaign_character(
+            r#"{"id":"char-1","name":"Nyx","level":3,"class":"rogue"}"#,
+        )
+        .unwrap();
+        let event = parse_campaign_event(
+            r#"{"id":"evt-1","kind":"note","summary":"Nyx scouts the goblin trail."}"#,
+        )
+        .unwrap();
+
+        assert_eq!(
+            campaign_json(&campaign),
+            r#"{"id":"camp-1","name":"Lost Mine","dm":"dm"}"#
+        );
+        assert_eq!(
+            campaign_character_json(&character),
+            r#"{"id":"char-1","name":"Nyx","level":3,"class":"rogue"}"#
+        );
+        assert_eq!(
+            campaign_event_json(&event),
+            r#"{"id":"evt-1","kind":"note"}"#
+        );
+        assert_eq!(
+            campaign_state_json(&campaign, &[character], 1),
+            r#"{"id":"camp-1","name":"Lost Mine","dm":"dm","characters":[{"id":"char-1","name":"Nyx","level":3,"class":"rogue"}],"log_count":1}"#
+        );
+    }
+

+enum CampaignResult {
+    Ok(String),
+    BadRequest,
+    NotFound,
+    Conflict,
+    StorageError,
+}
+
+fn create_campaign(body: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CampaignResult {
+    let campaign = match parse_campaign(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CampaignResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if campaign_exists(storage, &campaign.id) {
+        return CampaignResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO campaigns (id, name, dm) VALUES ({}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&campaign.id),
+        sql_string(&campaign.name),
+        sql_string(&campaign.dm)
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CampaignResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_json(&campaign))
+}
+
+fn add_campaign_character(
+    campaign_id: &str,
+    body: &str,
+    storage: &Storage,
+) -> CampaignResult {
+    if !valid_record_id(campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    if !campaign_exists(storage, campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::NotFound;
+    }
+    let character = match parse_campaign_character(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CampaignResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if campaign_character_exists(storage, &character.id) {
+        return CampaignResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO campaign_characters (id, campaign_id, name, level, class_name) VALUES ({}, {}, {}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&character.id),
+        sql_string(campaign_id),
+        sql_string(&character.name),
+        character.level,
+        sql_string(&character.class_name)
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CampaignResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_character_json(&character))
+}
+
+fn add_campaign_event(campaign_id: &str, body: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CampaignResult {
+    if !valid_record_id(campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    if !campaign_exists(storage, campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::NotFound;
+    }
+    let event = match parse_campaign_event(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CampaignResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if campaign_event_exists(storage, &event.id) {
+        return CampaignResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO campaign_events (id, campaign_id, kind, summary) VALUES ({}, {}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&event.id),
+        sql_string(campaign_id),
+        sql_string(&event.kind),
+        sql_string(&event.summary)
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CampaignResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_event_json(&event))
+}
+
+fn read_campaign_state(campaign_id: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CampaignResult {
+    if !valid_record_id(campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    let campaign = match load_campaign(storage, campaign_id) {
+        Ok(Some(value)) => value,
+        Ok(None) => return CampaignResult::NotFound,
+        Err(_) => return CampaignResult::StorageError,
+    };
+    let characters = match load_campaign_characters(storage, campaign_id) {
+        Ok(value) => value,
+        Err(_) => return CampaignResult::StorageError,
+    };
+    let log_count = match campaign_log_count(storage, campaign_id) {
+        Ok(value) => value,
+        Err(_) => return CampaignResult::StorageError,
+    };
+    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_state_json(&campaign, &characters, log_count))
+}
+
+fn parse_campaign(body: &str) -> Option<Campaign> {
+    let id = json_string_field(body, "id")?;
+    if !valid_record_id(&id) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    Some(Campaign {
+        id,
+        name: non_empty_json_string(body, "name")?,
+        dm: non_empty_json_string(body, "dm")?,
+    })
+}
+
+fn parse_campaign_character(body: &str) -> Option<CampaignCharacter> {
+    let id = json_string_field(body, "id")?;
+    if !valid_record_id(&id) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    let level = json_i64_field(body, "level")?;
+    if !(1..=20).contains(&level) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    Some(CampaignCharacter {
+        id,
+        name: non_empty_json_string(body, "name")?,
+        level,
+        class_name: non_empty_json_string(body, "class")?,
+    })
+}
+
+fn parse_campaign_event(body: &str) -> Option<CampaignEvent> {
+    let id = json_string_field(body, "id")?;
+    if !valid_record_id(&id) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    Some(CampaignEvent {
+        id,
+        kind: non_empty_json_string(body, "kind")?,
+        summary: non_empty_json_string(body, "summary")?,
+    })
+}
+
+fn valid_record_id(id: &str) -> bool {
+    !id.is_empty()
+        && id
+            .bytes()
+            .all(|b| b.is_ascii_alphanumeric() || b == b'-' || b == b'_')
+}
+
+fn campaign_exists(storage: &Storage, id: &str) -> bool {
+    query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT id FROM campaigns WHERE id = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(id)
+        ),
+    )
+    .map(|out| !out.trim().is_empty())
+    .unwrap_or(false)
+}
+
+fn campaign_character_exists(storage: &Storage, id: &str) -> bool {
+    query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT id FROM campaign_characters WHERE id = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(id)
+        ),
+    )
+    .map(|out| !out.trim().is_empty())
+    .unwrap_or(false)
+}
+
+fn campaign_event_exists(storage: &Storage, id: &str) -> bool {
+    query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT id FROM campaign_events WHERE id = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(id)
+        ),
+    )
+    .map(|out| !out.trim().is_empty())
+    .unwrap_or(false)
+}
+
+fn load_campaign(storage: &Storage, id: &str) -> Result<Option<Campaign>, String> {
+    let out = query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT id, name, dm FROM campaigns WHERE id = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(id)
+        ),
+    )?;
+    let Some(line) = out.lines().next() else {
+        return Ok(None);
+    };
+    let fields = line.splitn(3, '\t').collect::<Vec<_>>();
+    if fields.len() != 3 {
+        return Err("malformed campaign row".to_string());
+    }
+    Ok(Some(Campaign {
+        id: fields[0].to_string(),
+        name: fields[1].to_string(),
+        dm: fields[2].to_string(),
+    }))
+}
+
+fn load_campaign_characters(
+    storage: &Storage,
+    campaign_id: &str,
+) -> Result<Vec<CampaignCharacter>, String> {
+    let out = query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT id, name, level, class_name FROM campaign_characters WHERE campaign_id = {} ORDER BY rowid;",
+            sql_string(campaign_id)
+        ),
+    )?;
+    let mut characters = Vec::new();
+    for line in out.lines() {
+        let fields = line.splitn(4, '\t').collect::<Vec<_>>();
+        if fields.len() != 4 {
+            return Err("malformed campaign character row".to_string());
+        }
+        characters.push(CampaignCharacter {
+            id: fields[0].to_string(),
+            name: fields[1].to_string(),
+            level: fields[2].parse().map_err(|_| "bad level")?,
+            class_name: fields[3].to_string(),
+        });
+    }
+    Ok(characters)
+}
+
+fn campaign_log_count(storage: &Storage, campaign_id: &str) -> Result<i64, String> {
+    let out = query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM campaign_events WHERE campaign_id = {};",
+            sql_string(campaign_id)
+        ),
+    )?;
+    out.trim().parse().map_err(|_| "bad log count".to_string())
+}
+
+fn campaign_json(campaign: &Campaign) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"id":"{}","name":"{}","dm":"{}"}}"#,
+        json_escape(&campaign.id),
+        json_escape(&campaign.name),
+        json_escape(&campaign.dm)
+    )
+}
+
+fn campaign_character_json(character: &CampaignCharacter) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"id":"{}","name":"{}","level":{},"class":"{}"}}"#,
+        json_escape(&character.id),
+        json_escape(&character.name),
+        character.level,
+        json_escape(&character.class_name)
+    )
+}
+
+fn campaign_event_json(event: &CampaignEvent) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"id":"{}","kind":"{}"}}"#,
+        json_escape(&event.id),
+        json_escape(&event.kind)
+    )
+}
+
+fn campaign_state_json(
+    campaign: &Campaign,
+    characters: &[CampaignCharacter],
+    log_count: i64,
+) -> String {
+    let character_json = characters
+        .iter()
+        .map(campaign_character_json)
+        .collect::<Vec<_>>()
+        .join(",");
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"id":"{}","name":"{}","dm":"{}","characters":[{}],"log_count":{}}}"#,
+        json_escape(&campaign.id),
+        json_escape(&campaign.name),
+        json_escape(&campaign.dm),
+        character_json,
+        log_count
+    )
+}

     #[test]
+    fn campaign_json_matches_contract() {
+        let campaign =
+            parse_campaign(r#"{"id":"camp-1","name":"Lost Mine","dm":"dm"}"#).unwrap();
+        let character = parse_campaign_character(
+            r#"{"id":"char-1","name":"Nyx","level":3,"class":"rogue"}"#,
+        )
+        .unwrap();
+        let event = parse_campaign_event(
+            r#"{"id":"evt-1","kind":"note","summary":"Nyx scouts the goblin trail."}"#,
+        )
+        .unwrap();
+

+            campaign_json(&campaign),
+            r#"{"id":"camp-1","name":"Lost Mine","dm":"dm"}"#
+        );

+            campaign_character_json(&character),
+            r#"{"id":"char-1","name":"Nyx","level":3,"class":"rogue"}"#
+        );
+        assert_eq!(
+            campaign_event_json(&event),
+            r#"{"id":"evt-1","kind":"note"}"#
+        );
+        assert_eq!(
+            campaign_state_json(&campaign, &[character], 1),
+            r#"{"id":"camp-1","name":"Lost Mine","dm":"dm","characters":[{"id":"char-1","name":"Nyx","level":3,"class":"rogue"}],"log_count":1}"#
+        );
+    }

    91	fn main() -> std::io::Result<()> {
    92	    let port = env::var("PORT").unwrap_or_else(|_| "8080".to_string());
    93	    let storage = Arc::new(Mutex::new(Storage {

   100	    let users = Arc::new(Mutex::new(load_users(&storage.lock().unwrap())));
   101	    let listener = TcpListener::bind(format!("127.0.0.1:{port}"))?;
   102	    for stream in listener.incoming() {
   103	        if let Ok(mut stream) = stream {
   104	            let _ = handle(&mut stream, &sessions, &users, &storage);
   105	        }
   106	    }
   107	    Ok(())
   108	}

   110	fn handle(
   111	    stream: &mut TcpStream,
   112	    sessions: &Sessions,
   113	    users: &Users,
   114	    storage: &StorageState,
   115	) -> std::io::Result<()> {
   116	    let req = read_request(stream)?;
   117	    let (head, body) = split_request(&req);
   118	    let first = head.lines().next().unwrap_or("");
   119	    let mut parts = first.split_whitespace();
   120	    let method = parts.next().unwrap_or("");
   121	    let path = parts.next().unwrap_or("");
   122	
   123	    match (method, path) {
   124	        ("GET", "/health") => respond(stream, 200, r#"{"ok":true}"#),
   125	        ("GET", "/v1/storage/status") => {

   515	fn sql_string(value: &str) -> String {
   516	    format!("'{}'", value.replace('\'', "''"))

   518	
   519	fn encode_session(session: &CombatSession) -> String {
   520	    let combatants = session
   521	        .order
   522	        .iter()
   523	        .map(|combatant| {
   524	            let conditions = combatant
   525	                .conditions
   526	                .iter()
   527	                .map(|condition| {
   528	                    format!(
   529	                        "{}:{}",
   530	                        hex_encode(&condition.condition),
   531	                        condition.remaining_rounds
   532	                    )
   533	                })
   534	                .collect::<Vec<_>>()
   535	                .join("~");
   536	            format!(
   537	                "{},{},{},{},{}",
   538	                hex_encode(&combatant.name),
   539	                combatant.dex,
   540	                combatant.score,
   541	                if combatant.had_conditions { 1 } else { 0 },
   542	                conditions
   543	            )
   544	        })
   545	        .collect::<Vec<_>>()
   546	        .join(";");
   547	    format!(
   548	        "{}|{}|{}|{}",
   549	        hex_encode(&session.id),
   550	        session.round,
   551	        session.turn_index,
   552	        combatants
   553	    )
   554	}
   555	
   556	fn decode_session(encoded: &str) -> Option<CombatSession> {
   557	    let mut parts = encoded.splitn(4, '|');
   558	    let id = hex_decode(parts.next()?)?;
   559	    let round = parts.next()?.parse().ok()?;
   560	    let turn_index = parts.next()?.parse().ok()?;
   561	    let mut order = Vec::new();
   562	    for combatant_text in parts.next()?.split(';') {
   563	        if combatant_text.is_empty() {
   564	            continue;
   565	        }
   566	        let fields = combatant_text.splitn(5, ',').collect::<Vec<_>>();
   567	        if fields.len() != 5 {
   568	            return None;
   569	        }
   570	        let mut conditions = Vec::new();
   571	        if !fields[4].is_empty() {
   572	            for condition_text in fields[4].split('~') {
   573	                let (name, remaining) = condition_text.split_once(':')?;
   574	                conditions.push(Condition {
   575	                    condition: hex_decode(name)?,
   576	                    remaining_rounds: remaining.parse().ok()?,
   577	                });
   578	            }
   579	        }
   580	        order.push(Combatant {
   581	            name: hex_decode(fields[0])?,
   582	            dex: fields[1].parse().ok()?,
   583	            score: fields[2].parse().ok()?,
   584	            had_conditions: fields[3] == "1",
   585	            conditions,
   586	        });
   587	    }
   588	    if order.is_empty() || turn_index >= order.len() {
   589	        return None;
   590	    }
   591	    Some(CombatSession {
   592	        id,
   593	        round,
   594	        turn_index,
   595	        order,
   596	    })
   597	}
   598	
   599	fn hex_encode(value: &str) -> String {
   600	    let mut out = String::new();
   601	    for byte in value.as_bytes() {
   602	        out.push_str(&format!("{byte:02x}"));
   603	    }
   604	    out
   605	}
   606	
   607	fn hex_decode(value: &str) -> Option<String> {
   608	    if !value.len().is_multiple_of(2) {
   609	        return None;
   610	    }
   611	    let mut bytes = Vec::new();
   612	    let mut i = 0;
   613	    while i < value.len() {
   614	        bytes.push(u8::from_str_radix(&value[i..i + 2], 16).ok()?);
   615	        i += 2;
   616	    }
   617	    String::from_utf8(bytes).ok()
   618	}
   619	
   620	fn read_request(stream: &mut TcpStream) -> std::io::Result<String> {
   621	    let mut bytes = Vec::new();
   622	    let mut buf = [0_u8; 4096];
   623	    loop {
   624	        let n = stream.read(&mut buf)?;
   625	        if n == 0 {
   626	            break;
   627	        }
   628	        bytes.extend_from_slice(&buf[..n]);
   629	        if let Some(header_end) = find_bytes(&bytes, b"\r\n\r\n") {
   630	            let head = String::from_utf8_lossy(&bytes[..header_end]);
   631	            let content_len = content_length(&head).unwrap_or(0);
   632	            if bytes.len() >= header_end + 4 + content_len {
   633	                break;
   634	            }
   635	        }
   636	    }
   637	    Ok(String::from_utf8_lossy(&bytes).into_owned())
   638	}
   639	
   640	fn find_bytes(haystack: &[u8], needle: &[u8]) -> Option<usize> {
   641	    haystack.windows(needle.len()).position(|w| w == needle)
   642	}
   643	
   644	fn content_length(head: &str) -> Option<usize> {
   645	    for line in head.lines() {
   646	        if let Some((name, value)) = line.split_once(':') {
   647	            if name.eq_ignore_ascii_case("content-length") {
   648	                return value.trim().parse().ok();
   649	            }
   650	        }
   651	    }
   652	    None
   653	}
   654	
   655	fn split_request(req: &str) -> (&str, &str) {
   656	    match req.split_once("\r\n\r\n") {
   657	        Some((head, body)) => (head, body),
   658	        None => (req, ""),
   659	    }
   660	}
   661	
   662	fn dice_stats(body: &str) -> Option<String> {
   663	    let expression = json_string_field(body, "expression")?;
   664	    let (dice_count, sides, modifier) = parse_dice(&expression)?;
   665	    let min = dice_count + modifier;
   666	    let max = dice_count * sides + modifier;
   667	    let average_twice = dice_count * (sides + 1) + 2 * modifier;
   668	    let average = number_from_halves(average_twice);
   669	    Some(format!(
   670	        r#"{{"dice_count":{dice_count},"sides":{sides},"modifier":{modifier},"min":{min},"max":{max},"average":{average}}}"#
   671	    ))
   672	}
   673	
   674	fn parse_dice(expression: &str) -> Option<(i64, i64, i64)> {
   675	    let d = expression.find('d')?;
   676	    let count: i64 = expression[..d].parse().ok()?;
   677	    let rest = &expression[d + 1..];
   678	    let split = rest.find(['+', '-']);
   679	    let (sides_text, modifier) = match split {
   680	        Some(i) => {
   681	            let sides_text = &rest[..i];
   682	            let sign = rest.as_bytes()[i] as char;
   683	            let value: i64 = rest[i + 1..].parse().ok()?;
   684	            (sides_text, if sign == '-' { -value } else { value })
   685	        }
   686	        None => (rest, 0),
   687	    };
   688	    let sides: i64 = sides_text.parse().ok()?;
   689	    if count > 0 && sides > 0 {
   690	        Some((count, sides, modifier))
   691	    } else {
   692	        None
   693	    }
   694	}
   695	
   696	fn ability_check(body: &str) -> Option<String> {
   697	    let roll = json_i64_field(body, "roll")?;
   698	    let modifier = json_i64_field(body, "modifier")?;
   699	    let dc = json_i64_field(body, "dc")?;
   700	    let total = roll + modifier;
   701	    let success = total >= dc;
   702	    let margin = total - dc;
   703	    Some(format!(
   704	        r#"{{"total":{total},"success":{success},"margin":{margin}}}"#
   705	    ))
   706	}
   707	
   708	fn adjusted_xp(body: &str) -> Option<String> {
   709	    let party = json_array_field(body, "party")?;
   710	    let monsters = json_array_field(body, "monsters")?;
   711	
   712	    let mut easy = 0_i64;
   713	    let mut medium = 0_i64;
   714	    let mut hard = 0_i64;
   715	    let mut deadly = 0_i64;
   716	    for member in array_objects(party) {
   717	        match json_i64_field(member, "level")? {
   718	            3 => {
   719	                easy += 75;
   720	                medium += 150;
   721	                hard += 225;
   722	                deadly += 400;
   723	            }
   724	            _ => return None,
   725	        }
   726	    }
   727	
   728	    let mut base_xp = 0_i64;
   729	    let mut monster_count = 0_i64;
   730	    for monster in array_objects(monsters) {
   731	        let cr = json_string_field(monster, "cr")?;
   732	        let count = json_i64_field(monster, "count")?;
   733	        if count < 0 {
   734	            return None;
   735	        }
   736	        base_xp += cr_xp(&cr)? * count;
   737	        monster_count += count;
   738	    }
   739	
   740	    let multiplier_twice = monster_multiplier_twice(monster_count);
   741	    let adjusted_twice = base_xp * multiplier_twice;
   742	    let adjusted_for_compare = adjusted_twice;
   743	    let difficulty = if adjusted_for_compare >= deadly * 2 {
   744	        "deadly"
   745	    } else if adjusted_for_compare >= hard * 2 {
   746	        "hard"
   747	    } else if adjusted_for_compare >= medium * 2 {
   748	        "medium"
   749	    } else if adjusted_for_compare >= easy * 2 {
   750	        "easy"
   751	    } else {
   752	        "trivial"
   753	    };
   754	    let multiplier = number_from_halves(multiplier_twice);
   755	    let adjusted = number_from_halves(adjusted_twice);
   756	
   757	    Some(format!(
   758	        r#"{{"base_xp":{base_xp},"monster_count":{monster_count},"multiplier":{multiplier},"adjusted_xp":{adjusted},"difficulty":"{difficulty}","thresholds":{{"easy":{easy},"medium":{medium},"hard":{hard},"deadly":{deadly}}}}}"#
   759	    ))
   760	}
   761	
   762	fn cr_xp(cr: &str) -> Option<i64> {
   763	    match cr {
   764	        "0" => Some(10),
   765	        "1/8" => Some(25),
   766	        "1/4" => Some(50),
   767	        "1/2" => Some(100),
   768	        "1" => Some(200),
   769	        "2" => Some(450),
   770	        "3" => Some(700),
   771	        "4" => Some(1100),
   772	        "5" => Some(1800),
   773	        _ => None,
   774	    }
   775	}
   776	
   777	fn monster_multiplier_twice(count: i64) -> i64 {
   778	    match count {
   779	        1 => 2,
   780	        2 => 3,
   781	        3..=6 => 4,
   782	        7..=10 => 5,
   783	        11..=14 => 6,
   784	        15.. => 8,
   785	        _ => 2,
   786	    }
   787	}
   788	
   789	fn initiative_order(body: &str) -> Option<String> {
   790	    let combatants = json_array_field(body, "combatants")?;
   791	    let mut rows = Vec::new();
   792	    for combatant in array_objects(combatants) {
   793	        let name = json_string_field(combatant, "name")?;
   794	        let dex = json_i64_field(combatant, "dex")?;
   795	        let roll = json_i64_field(combatant, "roll")?;
   796	        rows.push((name, dex, roll + dex));
   797	    }
   798	    rows.sort_by(|a, b| {
   799	        b.2.cmp(&a.2)
   800	            .then_with(|| b.1.cmp(&a.1))
   801	            .then_with(|| a.0.cmp(&b.0))
   802	    });
   803	
   804	    let entries: Vec<String> = rows
   805	        .into_iter()
   806	        .map(|(name, _, score)| format!(r#"{{"name":"{}","score":{score}}}"#, json_escape(&name)))
   807	        .collect();
   808	    Some(format!(r#"{{"order":[{}]}}"#, entries.join(",")))
   809	}

  1711	fn json_string_field(source: &str, key: &str) -> Option<String> {
  1712	    let value = field_value(source, key)?;
  1713	    let bytes = value.as_bytes();
  1714	    if bytes.first().copied()? != b'"' {
  1715	        return None;
  1716	    }
  1717	    let mut out = String::new();
  1718	    let mut escaped = false;
  1719	    for (i, ch) in value[1..].char_indices() {
  1720	        if escaped {
  1721	            match ch {
  1722	                '"' | '\\' | '/' => out.push(ch),
  1723	                'n' => out.push('\n'),
  1724	                'r' => out.push('\r'),
  1725	                't' => out.push('\t'),
  1726	                'b' => out.push('\u{0008}'),
  1727	                'f' => out.push('\u{000c}'),
  1728	                _ => return None,
  1729	            }
  1730	            escaped = false;
  1731	        } else if ch == '\\' {
  1732	            escaped = true;
  1733	        } else if ch == '"' {
  1734	            return Some(out);
  1735	        } else {
  1736	            out.push(ch);
  1737	        }
  1738	        let _ = i;
  1739	    }
  1740	    None
  1741	}
  1742	
  1743	fn json_i64_field(source: &str, key: &str) -> Option<i64> {

  1745	    let mut end = 0;

+enum CampaignResult {
+    Ok(String),
+    BadRequest,
+    NotFound,
+    Conflict,
+    StorageError,
+}
+
+fn create_campaign(body: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CampaignResult {
+    let campaign = match parse_campaign(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CampaignResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if campaign_exists(storage, &campaign.id) {
+        return CampaignResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO campaigns (id, name, dm) VALUES ({}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&campaign.id),
+        sql_string(&campaign.name),
+        sql_string(&campaign.dm)
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CampaignResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_json(&campaign))
+}
+
+fn add_campaign_character(
+    campaign_id: &str,
+    body: &str,
+    storage: &Storage,
+) -> CampaignResult {
+    if !valid_record_id(campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    if !campaign_exists(storage, campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::NotFound;
+    }
+    let character = match parse_campaign_character(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CampaignResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if campaign_character_exists(storage, &character.id) {
+        return CampaignResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO campaign_characters (id, campaign_id, name, level, class_name) VALUES ({}, {}, {}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&character.id),
+        sql_string(campaign_id),
+        sql_string(&character.name),
+        character.level,
+        sql_string(&character.class_name)
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CampaignResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_character_json(&character))
+}
+
+fn add_campaign_event(campaign_id: &str, body: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CampaignResult {
+    if !valid_record_id(campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    if !campaign_exists(storage, campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::NotFound;
+    }
+    let event = match parse_campaign_event(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CampaignResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if campaign_event_exists(storage, &event.id) {
+        return CampaignResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO campaign_events (id, campaign_id, kind, summary) VALUES ({}, {}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&event.id),
+        sql_string(campaign_id),
+        sql_string(&event.kind),
+        sql_string(&event.summary)
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CampaignResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_event_json(&event))
+}
+
+fn read_campaign_state(campaign_id: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CampaignResult {
+    if !valid_record_id(campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    let campaign = match load_campaign(storage, campaign_id) {
+        Ok(Some(value)) => value,
+        Ok(None) => return CampaignResult::NotFound,
+        Err(_) => return CampaignResult::StorageError,
+    };
+    let characters = match load_campaign_characters(storage, campaign_id) {
+        Ok(value) => value,
+        Err(_) => return CampaignResult::StorageError,
+    };
+    let log_count = match campaign_log_count(storage, campaign_id) {
+        Ok(value) => value,
+        Err(_) => return CampaignResult::StorageError,
+    };
+    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_state_json(&campaign, &characters, log_count))
+}
+
+fn parse_campaign(body: &str) -> Option<Campaign> {
+    let id = json_string_field(body, "id")?;
+    if !valid_record_id(&id) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    Some(Campaign {
+        id,
+        name: non_empty_json_string(body, "name")?,
+        dm: non_empty_json_string(body, "dm")?,
+    })
+}
+
+fn parse_campaign_character(body: &str) -> Option<CampaignCharacter> {
+    let id = json_string_field(body, "id")?;
+    if !valid_record_id(&id) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    let level = json_i64_field(body, "level")?;
+    if !(1..=20).contains(&level) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    Some(CampaignCharacter {
+        id,
+        name: non_empty_json_string(body, "name")?,
+        level,
+        class_name: non_empty_json_string(body, "class")?,
+    })
+}
+
+fn parse_campaign_event(body: &str) -> Option<CampaignEvent> {
+    let id = json_string_field(body, "id")?;
+    if !valid_record_id(&id) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    Some(CampaignEvent {
+        id,
+        kind: non_empty_json_string(body, "kind")?,
+        summary: non_empty_json_string(body, "summary")?,
+    })
+}
+
+fn valid_record_id(id: &str) -> bool {
+    !id.is_empty()
+        && id
+            .bytes()
+            .all(|b| b.is_ascii_alphanumeric() || b == b'-' || b == b'_')
+}
+
+fn campaign_exists(storage: &Storage, id: &str) -> bool {
+    query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT id FROM campaigns WHERE id = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(id)
+        ),
+    )
+    .map(|out| !out.trim().is_empty())
+    .unwrap_or(false)
+}
+
+fn campaign_character_exists(storage: &Storage, id: &str) -> bool {
+    query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT id FROM campaign_characters WHERE id = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(id)
+        ),
+    )
+    .map(|out| !out.trim().is_empty())
+    .unwrap_or(false)
+}
+
+fn campaign_event_exists(storage: &Storage, id: &str) -> bool {
+    query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT id FROM campaign_events WHERE id = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(id)
+        ),
+    )
+    .map(|out| !out.trim().is_empty())
+    .unwrap_or(false)
+}
+
+fn load_campaign(storage: &Storage, id: &str) -> Result<Option<Campaign>, String> {
+    let out = query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT id, name, dm FROM campaigns WHERE id = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(id)
+        ),
+    )?;
+    let Some(line) = out.lines().next() else {
+        return Ok(None);
+    };
+    let fields = line.splitn(3, '\t').collect::<Vec<_>>();
+    if fields.len() != 3 {
+        return Err("malformed campaign row".to_string());
+    }
+    Ok(Some(Campaign {
+        id: fields[0].to_string(),
+        name: fields[1].to_string(),
+        dm: fields[2].to_string(),
+    }))
+}
+
+fn load_campaign_characters(
+    storage: &Storage,
+    campaign_id: &str,
+) -> Result<Vec<CampaignCharacter>, String> {
+    let out = query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT id, name, level, class_name FROM campaign_characters WHERE campaign_id = {} ORDER BY rowid;",
+            sql_string(campaign_id)
+        ),
+    )?;
+    let mut characters = Vec::new();
+    for line in out.lines() {
+        let fields = line.splitn(4, '\t').collect::<Vec<_>>();
+        if fields.len() != 4 {
+            return Err("malformed campaign character row".to_string());
+        }
+        characters.push(CampaignCharacter {
+            id: fields[0].to_string(),
+            name: fields[1].to_string(),
+            level: fields[2].parse().map_err(|_| "bad level")?,
+            class_name: fields[3].to_string(),
+        });
+    }
+    Ok(characters)
+}
+
+fn campaign_log_count(storage: &Storage, campaign_id: &str) -> Result<i64, String> {
+    let out = query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM campaign_events WHERE campaign_id = {};",
+            sql_string(campaign_id)
+        ),
+    )?;
+    out.trim().parse().map_err(|_| "bad log count".to_string())
+}
+
+fn campaign_json(campaign: &Campaign) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"id":"{}","name":"{}","dm":"{}"}}"#,
+        json_escape(&campaign.id),
+        json_escape(&campaign.name),
+        json_escape(&campaign.dm)
+    )
+}
+
+fn campaign_character_json(character: &CampaignCharacter) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"id":"{}","name":"{}","level":{},"class":"{}"}}"#,
+        json_escape(&character.id),
+        json_escape(&character.name),
+        character.level,
+        json_escape(&character.class_name)
+    )
+}
+
+fn campaign_event_json(event: &CampaignEvent) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"id":"{}","kind":"{}"}}"#,
+        json_escape(&event.id),
+        json_escape(&event.kind)
+    )
+}
+
+fn campaign_state_json(
+    campaign: &Campaign,
+    characters: &[CampaignCharacter],
+    log_count: i64,
+) -> String {
+    let character_json = characters
+        .iter()
+        .map(campaign_character_json)
+        .collect::<Vec<_>>()
+        .join(",");
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"id":"{}","name":"{}","dm":"{}","characters":[{}],"log_count":{}}}"#,
+        json_escape(&campaign.id),
+        json_escape(&campaign.name),
+        json_escape(&campaign.dm),
+        character_json,
+        log_count
+    )
+}

     let monster = match parse_monster(body) {
         Some(value) => value,

     #[test]
+    fn campaign_json_matches_contract() {
+        let campaign =
+            parse_campaign(r#"{"id":"camp-1","name":"Lost Mine","dm":"dm"}"#).unwrap();
+        let character = parse_campaign_character(
+            r#"{"id":"char-1","name":"Nyx","level":3,"class":"rogue"}"#,
+        )
+        .unwrap();
+        let event = parse_campaign_event(
+            r#"{"id":"evt-1","kind":"note","summary":"Nyx scouts the goblin trail."}"#,
+        )
+        .unwrap();
+
+        assert_eq!(
+            campaign_json(&campaign),
+            r#"{"id":"camp-1","name":"Lost Mine","dm":"dm"}"#
+        );
+        assert_eq!(
+            campaign_character_json(&character),
+            r#"{"id":"char-1","name":"Nyx","level":3,"class":"rogue"}"#
+        );

+            campaign_event_json(&event),
+            r#"{"id":"evt-1","kind":"note"}"#

+            campaign_state_json(&campaign, &[character], 1),
+            r#"{"id":"camp-1","name":"Lost Mine","dm":"dm","characters":[{"id":"char-1","name":"Nyx","level":3,"class":"rogue"}],"log_count":1}"#
+        );
+    }

   889	    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_character_json(&character))
   890	}
   891	
   892	fn add_campaign_event(campaign_id: &str, body: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CampaignResult {
   893	    if !valid_record_id(campaign_id) {
   894	        return CampaignResult::BadRequest;
   895	    }
   896	    if !campaign_exists(storage, campaign_id) {
   897	        return CampaignResult::NotFound;
   898	    }
   899	    let event = match parse_campaign_event(body) {
   900	        Some(value) => value,
   901	        None => return CampaignResult::BadRequest,
   902	    };
   903	    if campaign_event_exists(storage, &event.id) {
   904	        return CampaignResult::Conflict;
   905	    }
   906	    let sql = format!(
   907	        "INSERT INTO campaign_events (id, campaign_id, kind, summary) VALUES ({}, {}, {}, {});",
   908	        sql_string(&event.id),
   909	        sql_string(campaign_id),
   910	        sql_string(&event.kind),
   911	        sql_string(&event.summary)
   912	    );
   913	    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
   914	        return CampaignResult::StorageError;
   915	    }
   916	    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_event_json(&event))
   917	}
   918	
   919	fn read_campaign_state(campaign_id: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CampaignResult {
   920	    if !valid_record_id(campaign_id) {
   921	        return CampaignResult::BadRequest;
   922	    }
   923	    let campaign = match load_campaign(storage, campaign_id) {
   924	        Ok(Some(value)) => value,
   925	        Ok(None) => return CampaignResult::NotFound,
   926	        Err(_) => return CampaignResult::StorageError,
   927	    };
   928	    let characters = match load_campaign_characters(storage, campaign_id) {
   929	        Ok(value) => value,
   930	        Err(_) => return CampaignResult::StorageError,
   931	    };
   932	    let log_count = match campaign_log_count(storage, campaign_id) {
   933	        Ok(value) => value,
   934	        Err(_) => return CampaignResult::StorageError,
   935	    };
   936	    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_state_json(&campaign, &characters, log_count))
   937	}
   938	
   939	fn parse_campaign(body: &str) -> Option<Campaign> {
   940	    let id = json_string_field(body, "id")?;
   941	    if !valid_record_id(&id) {
   942	        return None;
   943	    }
   944	    Some(Campaign {
   945	        id,
   946	        name: non_empty_json_string(body, "name")?,
   947	        dm: non_empty_json_string(body, "dm")?,
   948	    })
   949	}
   950	
   951	fn parse_campaign_character(body: &str) -> Option<CampaignCharacter> {
   952	    let id = json_string_field(body, "id")?;
   953	    if !valid_record_id(&id) {
   954	        return None;
   955	    }
   956	    let level = json_i64_field(body, "level")?;
   957	    if !(1..=20).contains(&level) {
   958	        return None;
   959	    }
   960	    Some(CampaignCharacter {
   961	        id,
   962	        name: non_empty_json_string(body, "name")?,
   963	        level,
   964	        class_name: non_empty_json_string(body, "class")?,
   965	    })
   966	}
   967	
   968	fn parse_campaign_event(body: &str) -> Option<CampaignEvent> {
   969	    let id = json_string_field(body, "id")?;
   970	    if !valid_record_id(&id) {
   971	        return None;
   972	    }
   973	    Some(CampaignEvent {
   974	        id,
   975	        kind: non_empty_json_string(body, "kind")?,
   976	        summary: non_empty_json_string(body, "summary")?,
   977	    })
   978	}

   980	fn valid_record_id(id: &str) -> bool {
   981	    !id.is_empty()
   982	        && id
   983	            .bytes()
   984	            .all(|b| b.is_ascii_alphanumeric() || b == b'-' || b == b'_')
   985	}

   987	fn campaign_exists(storage: &Storage, id: &str) -> bool {
   988	    query_sql(
   989	        storage,
   990	        &format!(
   991	            "SELECT id FROM campaigns WHERE id = {} LIMIT 1;",
   992	            sql_string(id)
   993	        ),
   994	    )
   995	    .map(|out| !out.trim().is_empty())
   996	    .unwrap_or(false)
   997	}

  1022	
  1023	fn load_campaign(storage: &Storage, id: &str) -> Result<Option<Campaign>, String> {
  1024	    let out = query_sql(
  1025	        storage,
  1026	        &format!(
  1027	            "SELECT id, name, dm FROM campaigns WHERE id = {} LIMIT 1;",
  1028	            sql_string(id)
  1029	        ),
  1030	    )?;
  1031	    let Some(line) = out.lines().next() else {
  1032	        return Ok(None);
  1033	    };
  1034	    let fields = line.splitn(3, '\t').collect::<Vec<_>>();
  1035	    if fields.len() != 3 {
  1036	        return Err("malformed campaign row".to_string());
  1037	    }
  1038	    Ok(Some(Campaign {
  1039	        id: fields[0].to_string(),
  1040	        name: fields[1].to_string(),
  1041	        dm: fields[2].to_string(),
  1042	    }))
  1043	}
  1044	
  1045	fn load_campaign_characters(
  1046	    storage: &Storage,
  1047	    campaign_id: &str,
  1048	) -> Result<Vec<CampaignCharacter>, String> {
  1049	    let out = query_sql(
  1050	        storage,
  1051	        &format!(
  1052	            "SELECT id, name, level, class_name FROM campaign_characters WHERE campaign_id = {} ORDER BY rowid;",
  1053	            sql_string(campaign_id)
  1054	        ),
  1055	    )?;
  1056	    let mut characters = Vec::new();
  1057	    for line in out.lines() {
  1058	        let fields = line.splitn(4, '\t').collect::<Vec<_>>();
  1059	        if fields.len() != 4 {
  1060	            return Err("malformed campaign character row".to_string());
  1061	        }
  1062	        characters.push(CampaignCharacter {
  1063	            id: fields[0].to_string(),
  1064	            name: fields[1].to_string(),
  1065	            level: fields[2].parse().map_err(|_| "bad level")?,
  1066	            class_name: fields[3].to_string(),
  1067	        });
  1068	    }
  1069	    Ok(characters)
  1070	}
  1071	
  1072	fn campaign_log_count(storage: &Storage, campaign_id: &str) -> Result<i64, String> {
  1073	    let out = query_sql(
  1074	        storage,
  1075	        &format!(

+enum CampaignResult {
+    Ok(String),
+    BadRequest,
+    NotFound,
+    Conflict,
+    StorageError,
+}
+
+fn create_campaign(body: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CampaignResult {
+    let campaign = match parse_campaign(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CampaignResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if campaign_exists(storage, &campaign.id) {
+        return CampaignResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO campaigns (id, name, dm) VALUES ({}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&campaign.id),
+        sql_string(&campaign.name),
+        sql_string(&campaign.dm)
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CampaignResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_json(&campaign))
+}
+
+fn add_campaign_character(
+    campaign_id: &str,
+    body: &str,
+    storage: &Storage,
+) -> CampaignResult {
+    if !valid_record_id(campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    if !campaign_exists(storage, campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::NotFound;
+    }
+    let character = match parse_campaign_character(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CampaignResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if campaign_character_exists(storage, &character.id) {
+        return CampaignResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO campaign_characters (id, campaign_id, name, level, class_name) VALUES ({}, {}, {}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&character.id),
+        sql_string(campaign_id),
+        sql_string(&character.name),
+        character.level,
+        sql_string(&character.class_name)
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CampaignResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_character_json(&character))
+}
+
+fn add_campaign_event(campaign_id: &str, body: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CampaignResult {
+    if !valid_record_id(campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    if !campaign_exists(storage, campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::NotFound;
+    }
+    let event = match parse_campaign_event(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CampaignResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if campaign_event_exists(storage, &event.id) {
+        return CampaignResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO campaign_events (id, campaign_id, kind, summary) VALUES ({}, {}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&event.id),
+        sql_string(campaign_id),
+        sql_string(&event.kind),
+        sql_string(&event.summary)
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CampaignResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_event_json(&event))
+}
+
+fn read_campaign_state(campaign_id: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CampaignResult {
+    if !valid_record_id(campaign_id) {
+        return CampaignResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    let campaign = match load_campaign(storage, campaign_id) {
+        Ok(Some(value)) => value,
+        Ok(None) => return CampaignResult::NotFound,
+        Err(_) => return CampaignResult::StorageError,
+    };
+    let characters = match load_campaign_characters(storage, campaign_id) {
+        Ok(value) => value,
+        Err(_) => return CampaignResult::StorageError,
+    };
+    let log_count = match campaign_log_count(storage, campaign_id) {
+        Ok(value) => value,
+        Err(_) => return CampaignResult::StorageError,
+    };
+    CampaignResult::Ok(campaign_state_json(&campaign, &characters, log_count))
+}
+
+fn parse_campaign(body: &str) -> Option<Campaign> {
+    let id = json_string_field(body, "id")?;
+    if !valid_record_id(&id) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    Some(Campaign {
+        id,
+        name: non_empty_json_string(body, "name")?,
+        dm: non_empty_json_string(body, "dm")?,
+    })
+}
+
+fn parse_campaign_character(body: &str) -> Option<CampaignCharacter> {
+    let id = json_string_field(body, "id")?;
+    if !valid_record_id(&id) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    let level = json_i64_field(body, "level")?;
+    if !(1..=20).contains(&level) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    Some(CampaignCharacter {
+        id,
+        name: non_empty_json_string(body, "name")?,
+        level,
+        class_name: non_empty_json_string(body, "class")?,
+    })
+}
+
+fn parse_campaign_event(body: &str) -> Option<CampaignEvent> {
+    let id = json_string_field(body, "id")?;
+    if !valid_record_id(&id) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    Some(CampaignEvent {
+        id,
+        kind: non_empty_json_string(body, "kind")?,
+        summary: non_empty_json_string(body, "summary")?,
+    })
+}
+
+fn valid_record_id(id: &str) -> bool {
+    !id.is_empty()
+        && id
+            .bytes()
+            .all(|b| b.is_ascii_alphanumeric() || b == b'-' || b == b'_')
+}
+
+fn campaign_exists(storage: &Storage, id: &str) -> bool {
+    query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT id FROM campaigns WHERE id = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(id)
+        ),
+    )
+    .map(|out| !out.trim().is_empty())
+    .unwrap_or(false)
+}
+
+fn campaign_character_exists(storage: &Storage, id: &str) -> bool {
+    query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT id FROM campaign_characters WHERE id = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(id)
+        ),
+    )
+    .map(|out| !out.trim().is_empty())
+    .unwrap_or(false)
+}
+
+fn campaign_event_exists(storage: &Storage, id: &str) -> bool {
+    query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT id FROM campaign_events WHERE id = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(id)
+        ),
+    )
+    .map(|out| !out.trim().is_empty())
+    .unwrap_or(false)
+}
+
+fn load_campaign(storage: &Storage, id: &str) -> Result<Option<Campaign>, String> {
+    let out = query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT id, name, dm FROM campaigns WHERE id = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(id)
+        ),
+    )?;
+    let Some(line) = out.lines().next() else {
+        return Ok(None);
+    };
+    let fields = line.splitn(3, '\t').collect::<Vec<_>>();
+    if fields.len() != 3 {
+        return Err("malformed campaign row".to_string());
+    }
+    Ok(Some(Campaign {
+        id: fields[0].to_string(),
+        name: fields[1].to_string(),
+        dm: fields[2].to_string(),
+    }))
+}
+
+fn load_campaign_characters(
+    storage: &Storage,
+    campaign_id: &str,
+) -> Result<Vec<CampaignCharacter>, String> {
+    let out = query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT id, name, level, class_name FROM campaign_characters WHERE campaign_id = {} ORDER BY rowid;",
+            sql_string(campaign_id)
+        ),
+    )?;
+    let mut characters = Vec::new();
+    for line in out.lines() {
+        let fields = line.splitn(4, '\t').collect::<Vec<_>>();
+        if fields.len() != 4 {
+            return Err("malformed campaign character row".to_string());
+        }
+        characters.push(CampaignCharacter {
+            id: fields[0].to_string(),
+            name: fields[1].to_string(),
+            level: fields[2].parse().map_err(|_| "bad level")?,
+            class_name: fields[3].to_string(),
+        });
+    }
+    Ok(characters)
+}
+
+fn campaign_log_count(storage: &Storage, campaign_id: &str) -> Result<i64, String> {
+    let out = query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM campaign_events WHERE campaign_id = {};",
+            sql_string(campaign_id)
+        ),
+    )?;
+    out.trim().parse().map_err(|_| "bad log count".to_string())
+}
+
+fn campaign_json(campaign: &Campaign) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"id":"{}","name":"{}","dm":"{}"}}"#,
+        json_escape(&campaign.id),
+        json_escape(&campaign.name),
+        json_escape(&campaign.dm)
+    )
+}
+
+fn campaign_character_json(character: &CampaignCharacter) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"id":"{}","name":"{}","level":{},"class":"{}"}}"#,
+        json_escape(&character.id),
+        json_escape(&character.name),
+        character.level,
+        json_escape(&character.class_name)
+    )
+}
+
+fn campaign_event_json(event: &CampaignEvent) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"id":"{}","kind":"{}"}}"#,
+        json_escape(&event.id),
+        json_escape(&event.kind)
+    )
+}
+
+fn campaign_state_json(
+    campaign: &Campaign,
+    characters: &[CampaignCharacter],
+    log_count: i64,
+) -> String {
+    let character_json = characters
+        .iter()
+        .map(campaign_character_json)
+        .collect::<Vec<_>>()
+        .join(",");
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"id":"{}","name":"{}","dm":"{}","characters":[{}],"log_count":{}}}"#,
+        json_escape(&campaign.id),
+        json_escape(&campaign.name),
+        json_escape(&campaign.dm),
+        character_json,
+        log_count
+    )
+}
